# Fragments & Notes Pack MEGA — DepthPack MEGA

1200 short in-world documents to make exploration feel stuffed with small stories.

## DOC-0001 — Burned Memo (anxious)
**Found In:** Glimmerdeep

> I’m writing this fast.
> If you’re reading it, don’t do what I did.
>
> They said the trail was clear. It isn’t.
> Keep your light low, keep your mouth shut, and if you find **Silt-grit Seed** (ID 30329),
> don’t sell it to the first smile you see.
>
> There’s a mark on the third plank — chalk, not salt.

- **Design Use:** readable loot, rumor seed, or breadcrumb.

> I’m writing this fast.
> If you’re reading it, don’t do what I did.
>
> They said the trail was clear. It isn’t.
> Keep your light low, keep your mouth shut, and if you find **Cedar-scented Seed** (ID 30175),
> don’t sell it to the first smile you see.
>
> There’s a mark on the third plank — chalk, not salt.

- **Design Use:** readable loot, rumor seed, or breadcrumb.

> I’m writing this fast.
> If you’re reading it, don’t do what I did.
>
> They said the trail was clear. It isn’t.
> Keep your light low, keep your mouth shut, and if you find **Faded Gland** (ID 31172),
> don’t sell it to the first smile you see.
>
> There’s a mark on the third plank — chalk, not salt.

- **Design Use:** readable loot, rumor seed, or breadcrumb.

> don’t sell it to the first smile you see.
>
> There’s a mark on the third plank — chalk, not salt.

> Keep your light low, keep your mouth shut, and if you find **Pine-sap Sash of the Trail** (ID 32748),
> don’t sell it to the first smile you see.
>
> There’s a mark on the third plank — chalk, not salt.
